宇宙中存在著許多不同類型的恆星，其中一種特別的恆星因其獨特的變光特性而聞名。這類恆星的亮度會因為內部物理過程的變化而周期性地增亮或減暗。問題來了，這種因內部脹縮導致亮度變化的恆星稱為什麼？=There are many different types of stars in the universe, but one particular type is known for its unique property of dimming. These stars' brightness periodically brightens and dims due to changes in their internal physical processes. The question is, what is a star called when its brightness varies due to internal expansion and contraction? A:Variable Star
紅巨星=Red Giant
中子星=Neutron Star
變星=Variable Star
白矮星=White Dwarf
當我們觀察夜空中最亮的恆星時，我們實際上是在看到它們過去的樣子，因為光需要時間才能從恆星旅行到地球。這引出了一個有趣的問題：我們看到的是大約多久之前的太陽？=When we look at the brightest stars in the night sky, we're actually seeing them as they appeared in the past, because it takes time for light to travel from the stars to Earth. This raises an interesting question: approximately how long ago are we looking at the Sun? A:8 Minutes
